<s> it is said however that you were carried away by your emotions <\s>
<s> the story has been told here to day of your relations with this er mrs <\s>
<s> honeywill on that story both the defence and the plea for mercy were in effect based <\s>
<s> now what is that story <\s>
<s> it is that you a young man and she a young woman unhappily married had formed an attachment which you both say with what truth i am unable to gauge had not yet resulted in immoral relations but which you both admit was about to result in such relationship <\s>
<s> your counsel has made an attempt to palliate this on the ground that the woman is in what he describes i think as a hopeless position <\s>
<s> as to that i can express no opinion <\s>
<s> she is a married woman and the fact is patent that you committed this crime with the view of furthering an immoral design <\s>
<s> now however i might wish i am not able to justify to my conscience a plea for mercy which has a basis inimical to morality <\s>
<s> it is vitiated ab initio and would if successful free you for the completion of this immoral project <\s>
<s> your counsel has made an attempt to trace your offence back to what he seems to suggest is a defect in the marriage law he has made an attempt also to show that to punish you with further imprisonment would be unjust <\s>
<s> i do not follow him in these flights <\s>
<s> the law is what it is a majestic edifice sheltering all of us each stone of which rests on another <\s>
<s> i am concerned only with its administration <\s>
<s> the crime you have committed is a very serious one <\s>
<s> i cannot feel it in accordance with my duty to society to exercise the powers i have in your favour <\s>
<s> you will go to penal servitude for three years <\s>
<s> falder who throughout the judge's speech has looked at him steadily lets his head fall forward on his breast <\s>
<s> ruth starts up from her seat as he is taken out by the warders <\s>
<s> there is a bustle in court <\s>
<s> speaking to the reporters gentlemen of the press i think that the name of the female witness should not be reported <\s>
<s> the reporters bow their acquiescence <\s>
<s> to ruth who is staring in the direction in which falder has disappeared do you understand your name will not be mentioned <\s>
<s> pulling her sleeve the judge is speaking to you <\s>
<s> ruth turns stares at the judge and turns away <\s>
<s> i shall sit rather late to day <\s>
<s> call the next case <\s>
<s> to a warder put up john booley <\s>
<s> to cries of witnesses in the case of booley the curtain falls <\s>
<s> act iii scene i a prison <\s>
<s> a plainly furnished room with two large barred windows overlooking the prisoners exercise yard where men in yellow clothes marked with arrows and yellow brimless caps are seen in single file at a distance of four yards from each other walking rapidly on serpentine white lines marked on the concrete floor of the yard <\s>
<s> two warders in blue uniforms with peaked caps and swords are stationed amongst them <\s>
<s> the room has distempered walls a bookcase with numerous official looking books a cupboard between the windows a plan of the prison on the wall a writing table covered with documents <\s>
<s> it is christmas eve <\s>
<s> the governor a neat grave looking man with a trim fair moustache the eyes of a theorist and grizzled hair receding from the temples is standing close to this writing table looking at a sort of rough saw made out of a piece of metal <\s>
<s> the hand in which he holds it is gloved for two fingers are missing <\s>
<s> the chief warder wooder a tall thin military looking man of sixty with grey moustache and melancholy monkey like eyes stands very upright two paces from him <\s>
<s> with a faint abstracted smile queer looking affair mr <\s>
<s> where did you find it <\s>
<s> in his mattress sir <\s>
<s> haven't come across such a thing for two years now <\s>
<s> with curiosity had he any set plan <\s>
<s> he'd sawed his window bar about that much <\s>
<s> he holds up his thumb and finger a quarter of an inch apart the governor <\s>
<s> i'll see him this afternoon <\s>
<s> an old hand i think <\s>
<s> yes sir fourth spell of penal <\s>
<s> you'd think an old lag like him would have had more sense by now <\s>
<s> with pitying contempt occupied his mind he said <\s>
<s> breaking in and breaking out that's all they think about <\s>
<s> next him again there's that young fellow falder star class and next him old clipton <\s>
<s> i want to see him about his eyes <\s>
<s> curious thing sir they seem to know when there's one of these tries at escape going on <\s>
<s> it makes them restive there's a regular wave going through them just now <\s>
<s> meditatively odd things those waves <\s>
<s> turning to look at the prisoners exercising seem quiet enough out here <\s>
<s> that irishman o'cleary began banging on his door this morning <\s>
<s> little thing like that's quite enough to upset the whole lot <\s>
<s> they're just like dumb animals at times <\s>
<s> i've seen it with horses before thunder it'll run right through cavalry lines <\s>

<s> holding up the saw seen this miller <\s>
<s> do for the museum eh <\s>
<s> he goes to the cupboard and opens it displaying to view a number of quaint ropes hooks and metal tools with labels tied on them that'll do thanks mr <\s>
<s> saluting thank you sir <\s>
<s> he goes out the governor <\s>
<s> account for the state of the men last day or two miller <\s>
<s> seems going through the whole place <\s>
<s> i don't know of anything <\s>
<s> by the way will you dine with us on christmas day <\s>
<s> worries me to feel the men discontented <\s>
<s> gazing at the saw have to punish this poor devil <\s>
<s> can't help liking a man who tries to escape <\s>
<s> he places the saw in his pocket and locks the cupboard again the chaplain <\s>
<s> extraordinary perverted will power some of them <\s>
<s> nothing to be done till it's broken <\s>
<s> and not much afterwards i'm afraid <\s>
<s> ground too hard for golf <\s>

<s> visitor who's been seeing q 3007 asks to speak to you sir <\s>

<s> yes we have that privilege from here my office is being done up <\s>
<s> sitting down at his table now please <\s>
<s> dragging his eyes with difficulty from the window i wanted to say a word to you i shan't keep you long <\s>
<s> confidentially fact is i oughtn't to be here by rights <\s>
<s> his sister came to me he's got no father and mother and she was in some distress <\s>
<s> my husband won't let me go and see him she said says he's disgraced the family <\s>
<s> and his other sister she said is an invalid <\s>
<s> it is said however that you were carried away by your emotions <\s>
<s> the story has been told here to day of your relations with this er mrs <\s>
<s> honeywill on that story both the defence and the plea for mercy were in effect based <\s>
<s> now what is that story <\s>
<s> it is that you a young man and she a young woman unhappily married had formed an attachment which you both say with what truth i am unable to gauge had not yet resulted in immoral relations but which you both admit was about to result in such relationship <\s>
<s> your counsel has made an attempt to palliate this on the ground that the woman is in what he describes i think as a hopeless position <\s>
<s> as to that i can express no opinion <\s>
<s> she is a married woman and the fact is patent that you committed this crime with the view of furthering an immoral design <\s>
<s> now however i might wish i am not able to justify to my conscience a plea for mercy which has a basis inimical to morality <\s>
<s> it is vitiated ab initio and would if successful free you for the completion of this immoral project <\s>
<s> your counsel has made an attempt to trace your offence back to what he seems to suggest is a defect in the marriage law he has made an attempt also to show that to punish you with further imprisonment would be unjust <\s>
<s> i do not follow him in these flights <\s>
<s> the law is what it is a majestic edifice sheltering all of us each stone of which rests on another <\s>
<s> i am concerned only with its administration <\s>
<s> the crime you have committed is a very serious one <\s>
<s> i cannot feel it in accordance with my duty to society to exercise the powers i have in your favour <\s>
<s> you will go to penal servitude for three years <\s>
<s> falder who throughout the judge's speech has looked at him steadily lets his head fall forward on his breast <\s>
<s> ruth starts up from her seat as he is taken out by the warders <\s>
<s> there is a bustle in court <\s>
<s> speaking to the reporters gentlemen of the press i think that the name of the female witness should not be reported <\s>
<s> the reporters bow their acquiescence <\s>
<s> to ruth who is staring in the direction in which falder has disappeared do you understand your name will not be mentioned <\s>
<s> pulling her sleeve the judge is speaking to you <\s>

<s> act iii scene i a prison <\s>
<s> a plainly furnished room with two large barred windows overlooking the prisoners exercise yard where men in yellow clothes marked with arrows and yellow brimless caps are seen in single file at a distance of four yards from each other walking rapidly on serpentine white lines marked on the concrete floor of the yard <\s>

<s> your counsel has made an attempt to trace your offence back to what he seems to suggest is a defect in the marriage law he has made an attempt also to show that to punish you with further imprisonment would be unjust <\s>
<s> i do not follow him in these flights <\s>
<s> the law is what it is a majestic edifice sheltering all of us each stone of which rests on another <\s>
<s> i am concerned only with its administration <\s>
<s> the crime you have committed is a very serious one <\s>
<s> i cannot feel it in accordance with my duty to society to exercise the powers i have in your favour <\s>
<s> you will go to penal servitude for three years <\s>
<s> falder who throughout the judge's speech has looked at him steadily lets his head fall forward on his breast <\s>
<s> ruth starts up from her seat as he is taken out by the warders <\s>
<s> there is a bustle in court <\s>
<s> speaking to the reporters gentlemen of the press i think that the name of the female witness should not be reported <\s>
<s> the reporters bow their acquiescence <\s>
<s> to ruth who is staring in the direction in which falder has disappeared do you understand your name will not be mentioned <\s>
<s> pulling her sleeve the judge is speaking to you <\s>
<s> ruth turns stares at the judge and turns away <\s>
<s> i shall sit rather late to day <\s>
<s> call the next case <\s>
<s> to a warder put up john booley <\s>
<s> to cries of witnesses in the case of booley the curtain falls <\s>
<s> act iii scene i a prison <\s>
<s> a plainly furnished room with two large barred windows overlooking the prisoners exercise yard where men in yellow clothes marked with arrows and yellow brimless caps are seen in single file at a distance of four yards from each other walking rapidly on serpentine white lines marked on the concrete floor of the yard <\s>
<s> two warders in blue uniforms with peaked caps and swords are stationed amongst them <\s>
<s> the room has distempered walls a bookcase with numerous official looking books a cupboard between the windows a plan of the prison on the wall a writing table covered with documents <\s>
<s> it is christmas eve <\s>
<s> the governor a neat grave looking man with a trim fair moustache the eyes of a theorist and grizzled hair receding from the temples is standing close to this writing table looking at a sort of rough saw made out of a piece of metal <\s>
<s> the hand in which he holds it is gloved for two fingers are missing <\s>
<s> the chief warder wooder a tall thin military looking man of sixty with grey moustache and melancholy monkey like eyes stands very upright two paces from him <\s>
<s> with a faint abstracted smile queer looking affair mr <\s>
<s> where did you find it <\s>
<s> in his mattress sir <\s>
<s> haven't come across such a thing for two years now <\s>
<s> with curiosity had he any set plan <\s>
<s> he'd sawed his window bar about that much <\s>
<s> he holds up his thumb and finger a quarter of an inch apart the governor <\s>
<s> i'll see him this afternoon <\s>
<s> an old hand i think <\s>
<s> yes sir fourth spell of penal <\s>
<s> you'd think an old lag like him would have had more sense by now <\s>
<s> with pitying contempt occupied his mind he said <\s>
<s> breaking in and breaking out that's all they think about <\s>
<s> next him again there's that young fellow falder star class and next him old clipton <\s>
<s> i want to see him about his eyes <\s>
<s> curious thing sir they seem to know when there's one of these tries at escape going on <\s>
<s> it makes them restive there's a regular wave going through them just now <\s>
<s> meditatively odd things those waves <\s>
<s> turning to look at the prisoners exercising seem quiet enough out here <\s>
<s> that irishman o'cleary began banging on his door this morning <\s>
<s> little thing like that's quite enough to upset the whole lot <\s>
<s> they're just like dumb animals at times <\s>
<s> i've seen it with horses before thunder it'll run right through cavalry lines <\s>
<s> the prison chaplain has entered <\s>
<s> he is a dark haired ascetic man in clerical undress with a peculiarly steady tight lipped face and slow cultured speech <\s>
<s> holding up the saw seen this miller <\s>
<s> do for the museum eh <\s>
<s> he goes to the cupboard and opens it displaying to view a number of quaint ropes hooks and metal tools with labels tied on them that'll do thanks mr <\s>
<s> saluting thank you sir <\s>
<s> he goes out the governor <\s>
<s> account for the state of the men last day or two miller <\s>
<s> seems going through the whole place <\s>
<s> i don't know of anything <\s>
<s> by the way will you dine with us on christmas day <\s>
<s> worries me to feel the men discontented <\s>
<s> gazing at the saw have to punish this poor devil <\s>
<s> can't help liking a man who tries to escape <\s>
<s> he places the saw in his pocket and locks the cupboard again the chaplain <\s>
<s> extraordinary perverted will power some of them <\s>
<s> nothing to be done till it's broken <\s>
<s> and not much afterwards i'm afraid <\s>
<s> ground too hard for golf <\s>
<s> wooder comes in again <\s>
<s> visitor who's been seeing q 3007 asks to speak to you sir <\s>
<s> i told him it wasn't usual <\s>
<s> shall i put him off sir <\s>
<s> wooder motions to some one without and as the visitor comes in withdraws <\s>
<s> the visitor is cokeson who is attired in a thick overcoat to the knees woollen gloves and carries a top hat <\s>
<s> i'm sorry to trouble you <\s>
<s> i've been talking to the young man <\s>
<s> we have a good many here <\s>
<s> name of falder forgery <\s>
<s> producing a card and handing it to the governor firm of james and walter how <\s>
<s> well known in the law <\s>
<s> receiving the card with a faint smile what do you want to see me about sir <\s>
<s> suddenly seeing the prisoners at exercise why <\s>
<s> yes we have that privilege from here my office is being done up <\s>
<s> sitting down at his table now please <\s>
<s> dragging his eyes with difficulty from the window i wanted to say a word to you i shan't keep you long <\s>
<s> confidentially fact is i oughtn't to be here by rights <\s>
<s> his sister came to me he's got no father and mother and she was in some distress <\s>
<s> my husband won't let me go and see him she said says he's disgraced the family <\s>
<s> and his other sister she said is an invalid <\s>
<s> it is said however that you were carried away by your emotions <\s>
<s> the story has been told here to day of your relations with this er mrs <\s>
<s> honeywill on that story both the defence and the plea for mercy were in effect based <\s>
<s> now what is that story <\s>
<s> it is that you a young man and she a young woman unhappily married had formed an attachment which you both say with what truth i am unable to gauge had not yet resulted in immoral relations but which you both admit was about to result in such relationship <\s>

<s> dragging his eyes with difficulty from the window i wanted to say a word to you i shan't keep you long <\s>
<s> confidentially fact is i oughtn't to be here by rights <\s>
<s> his sister came to me he's got no father and mother and she was in some distress <\s>
<s> my husband won't let me go and see him she said says he's disgraced the family <\s>
<s> and his other sister she said is an invalid <\s>
<s> it is said however that you were carried away by your emotions <\s>
<s> the story has been told here to day of your relations with this er mrs <\s>
<s> honeywill on that story both the defence and the plea for mercy were in effect based <\s>
<s> now what is that story <\s>
<s> it is that you a young man and she a young woman unhappily married had formed an attachment which you both say with what truth i am unable to gauge had not yet resulted in immoral relations but which you both admit was about to result in such relationship <\s>
<s> your counsel has made an attempt to palliate this on the ground that the woman is in what he describes i think as a hopeless position <\s>
<s> as to that i can express no opinion <\s>
<s> she is a married woman and the fact is patent that you committed this crime with the view of furthering an immoral design <\s>
<s> now however i might wish i am not able to justify to my conscience a plea for mercy which has a basis inimical to morality <\s>
<s> it is vitiated ab initio and would if successful free you for the completion of this immoral project <\s>
<s> your counsel has made an attempt to trace your offence back to what he seems to suggest is a defect in the marriage law he has made an attempt also to show that to punish you with further imprisonment would be unjust <\s>
<s> i do not follow him in these flights <\s>
<s> the law is what it is a majestic edifice sheltering all of us each stone of which rests on another <\s>
<s> i am concerned only with its administration <\s>
<s> the crime you have committed is a very serious one <\s>
<s> i cannot feel it in accordance with my duty to society to exercise the powers i have in your favour <\s>
<s> you will go to penal servitude for three years <\s>
<s> falder who throughout the judge's speech has looked at him steadily lets his head fall forward on his breast <\s>
<s> ruth starts up from her seat as he is taken out by the warders <\s>
<s> there is a bustle in court <\s>
<s> speaking to the reporters gentlemen of the press i think that the name of the female witness should not be reported <\s>
<s> the reporters bow their acquiescence <\s>
<s> to ruth who is staring in the direction in which falder has disappeared do you understand your name will not be mentioned <\s>
<s> pulling her sleeve the judge is speaking to you <\s>

<s> act iii scene i a prison <\s>
<s> a plainly furnished room with two large barred windows overlooking the prisoners exercise yard where men in yellow clothes marked with arrows and yellow brimless caps are seen in single file at a distance of four yards from each other walking rapidly on serpentine white lines marked on the concrete floor of the yard <\s>
<s> two warders in blue uniforms with peaked caps and swords are stationed amongst them <\s>
<s> the room has distempered walls a bookcase with numerous official looking books a cupboard between the windows a plan of the prison on the wall a writing table covered with documents <\s>
<s> it is christmas eve <\s>
<s> the governor a neat grave looking man with a trim fair moustache the eyes of a theorist and grizzled hair receding from the temples is standing close to this writing table looking at a sort of rough saw made out of a piece of metal <\s>
<s> the hand in which he holds it is gloved for two fingers are missing <\s>

<s> speaking to the reporters gentlemen of the press i think that the name of the female witness should not be reported <\s>

<s> act iii scene i a prison <\s>
<s> a plainly furnished room with two large barred windows overlooking the prisoners exercise yard where men in yellow clothes marked with arrows and yellow brimless caps are seen in single file at a distance of four yards from each other walking rapidly on serpentine white lines marked on the concrete floor of the yard <\s>
<s> two warders in blue uniforms with peaked caps and swords are stationed amongst them <\s>
<s> the room has distempered walls a bookcase with numerous official looking books a cupboard between the windows a plan of the prison on the wall a writing table covered with documents <\s>
<s> it is christmas eve <\s>
<s> the governor a neat grave looking man with a trim fair moustache the eyes of a theorist and grizzled hair receding from the temples is standing close to this writing table looking at a sort of rough saw made out of a piece of metal <\s>
<s> the hand in which he holds it is gloved for two fingers are missing <\s>
<s> the chief warder wooder a tall thin military looking man of sixty with grey moustache and melancholy monkey like eyes stands very upright two paces from him <\s>
<s> with a faint abstracted smile queer looking affair mr <\s>
<s> where did you find it <\s>
<s> in his mattress sir <\s>
<s> haven't come across such a thing for two years now <\s>
<s> with curiosity had he any set plan <\s>
<s> he'd sawed his window bar about that much <\s>
<s> he holds up his thumb and finger a quarter of an inch apart the governor <\s>
<s> i'll see him this afternoon <\s>
<s> an old hand i think <\s>
<s> yes sir fourth spell of penal <\s>
<s> you'd think an old lag like him would have had more sense by now <\s>
<s> with pitying contempt occupied his mind he said <\s>
<s> breaking in and breaking out that's all they think about <\s>
<s> next him again there's that young fellow falder star class and next him old clipton <\s>
<s> i want to see him about his eyes <\s>
<s> curious thing sir they seem to know when there's one of these tries at escape going on <\s>
<s> it makes them restive there's a regular wave going through them just now <\s>
<s> meditatively odd things those waves <\s>
<s> turning to look at the prisoners exercising seem quiet enough out here <\s>
<s> that irishman o'cleary began banging on his door this morning <\s>
<s> little thing like that's quite enough to upset the whole lot <\s>
<s> they're just like dumb animals at times <\s>
<s> i've seen it with horses before thunder it'll run right through cavalry lines <\s>
<s> the prison chaplain has entered <\s>
<s> he is a dark haired ascetic man in clerical undress with a peculiarly steady tight lipped face and slow cultured speech <\s>
<s> holding up the saw seen this miller <\s>
<s> do for the museum eh <\s>
<s> he goes to the cupboard and opens it displaying to view a number of quaint ropes hooks and metal tools with labels tied on them that'll do thanks mr <\s>
<s> saluting thank you sir <\s>
<s> he goes out the governor <\s>
<s> account for the state of the men last day or two miller <\s>
<s> seems going through the whole place <\s>
<s> i don't know of anything <\s>
<s> by the way will you dine with us on christmas day <\s>
<s> worries me to feel the men discontented <\s>
<s> gazing at the saw have to punish this poor devil <\s>
<s> can't help liking a man who tries to escape <\s>
<s> he places the saw in his pocket and locks the cupboard again the chaplain <\s>
<s> extraordinary perverted will power some of them <\s>
<s> nothing to be done till it's broken <\s>
<s> and not much afterwards i'm afraid <\s>
<s> ground too hard for golf <\s>
<s> wooder comes in again <\s>
<s> visitor who's been seeing q 3007 asks to speak to you sir <\s>
<s> i told him it wasn't usual <\s>
<s> shall i put him off sir <\s>
<s> wooder motions to some one without and as the visitor comes in withdraws <\s>
<s> the visitor is cokeson who is attired in a thick overcoat to the knees woollen gloves and carries a top hat <\s>
<s> i'm sorry to trouble you <\s>
<s> i've been talking to the young man <\s>
<s> we have a good many here <\s>
<s> name of falder forgery <\s>
<s> producing a card and handing it to the governor firm of james and walter how <\s>
<s> well known in the law <\s>
<s> receiving the card with a faint smile what do you want to see me about sir <\s>
<s> suddenly seeing the prisoners at exercise why <\s>
<s> yes we have that privilege from here my office is being done up <\s>
<s> sitting down at his table now please <\s>
<s> dragging his eyes with difficulty from the window i wanted to say a word to you i shan't keep you long <\s>
<s> confidentially fact is i oughtn't to be here by rights <\s>
<s> his sister came to me he's got no father and mother and she was in some distress <\s>
<s> my husband won't let me go and see him she said says he's disgraced the family <\s>
<s> and his other sister she said is an invalid <\s>
<s> it is said however that you were carried away by your emotions <\s>
<s> the story has been told here to day of your relations with this er mrs <\s>
<s> honeywill on that story both the defence and the plea for mercy were in effect based <\s>
<s> now what is that story <\s>
<s> it is that you a young man and she a young woman unhappily married had formed an attachment which you both say with what truth i am unable to gauge had not yet resulted in immoral relations but which you both admit was about to result in such relationship <\s>
<s> your counsel has made an attempt to palliate this on the ground that the woman is in what he describes i think as a hopeless position <\s>
<s> as to that i can express no opinion <\s>
<s> she is a married woman and the fact is patent that you committed this crime with the view of furthering an immoral design <\s>
<s> now however i might wish i am not able to justify to my conscience a plea for mercy which has a basis inimical to morality <\s>
<s> it is vitiated ab initio and would if successful free you for the completion of this immoral project <\s>
<s> your counsel has made an attempt to trace your offence back to what he seems to suggest is a defect in the marriage law he has made an attempt also to show that to punish you with further imprisonment would be unjust <\s>
<s> i do not follow him in these flights <\s>
<s> the law is what it is a majestic edifice sheltering all of us each stone of which rests on another <\s>
<s> i am concerned only with its administration <\s>
<s> the crime you have committed is a very serious one <\s>
<s> i cannot feel it in accordance with my duty to society to exercise the powers i have in your favour <\s>
<s> you will go to penal servitude for three years <\s>
<s> falder who throughout the judge's speech has looked at him steadily lets his head fall forward on his breast <\s>
<s> ruth starts up from her seat as he is taken out by the warders <\s>
<s> there is a bustle in court <\s>

<s> wooder comes in again <\s>
<s> visitor who's been seeing q 3007 asks to speak to you sir <\s>
<s> i told him it wasn't usual <\s>
<s> shall i put him off sir <\s>
<s> wooder motions to some one without and as the visitor comes in withdraws <\s>
<s> the visitor is cokeson who is attired in a thick overcoat to the knees woollen gloves and carries a top hat <\s>
<s> i'm sorry to trouble you <\s>
<s> i've been talking to the young man <\s>
<s> we have a good many here <\s>
<s> name of falder forgery <\s>
<s> producing a card and handing it to the governor firm of james and walter how <\s>
<s> well known in the law <\s>
<s> receiving the card with a faint smile what do you want to see me about sir <\s>
<s> suddenly seeing the prisoners at exercise why <\s>
<s> yes we have that privilege from here my office is being done up <\s>
<s> sitting down at his table now please <\s>
<s> dragging his eyes with difficulty from the window i wanted to say a word to you i shan't keep you long <\s>
<s> confidentially fact is i oughtn't to be here by rights <\s>
<s> his sister came to me he's got no father and mother and she was in some distress <\s>
<s> my husband won't let me go and see him she said says he's disgraced the family <\s>
<s> and his other sister she said is an invalid <\s>
<s> it is said however that you were carried away by your emotions <\s>
<s> the story has been told here to day of your relations with this er mrs <\s>
<s> honeywill on that story both the defence and the plea for mercy were in effect based <\s>
<s> now what is that story <\s>
<s> it is that you a young man and she a young woman unhappily married had formed an attachment which you both say with what truth i am unable to gauge had not yet resulted in immoral relations but which you both admit was about to result in such relationship <\s>
<s> your counsel has made an attempt to palliate this on the ground that the woman is in what he describes i think as a hopeless position <\s>
<s> as to that i can express no opinion <\s>
<s> she is a married woman and the fact is patent that you committed this crime with the view of furthering an immoral design <\s>
<s> now however i might wish i am not able to justify to my conscience a plea for mercy which has a basis inimical to morality <\s>
<s> it is vitiated ab initio and would if successful free you for the completion of this immoral project <\s>
<s> your counsel has made an attempt to trace your offence back to what he seems to suggest is a defect in the marriage law he has made an attempt also to show that to punish you with further imprisonment would be unjust <\s>
<s> i do not follow him in these flights <\s>
<s> the law is what it is a majestic edifice sheltering all of us each stone of which rests on another <\s>
<s> i am concerned only with its administration <\s>
<s> the crime you have committed is a very serious one <\s>
<s> i cannot feel it in accordance with my duty to society to exercise the powers i have in your favour <\s>
<s> you will go to penal servitude for three years <\s>
<s> falder who throughout the judge's speech has looked at him steadily lets his head fall forward on his breast <\s>
<s> ruth starts up from her seat as he is taken out by the warders <\s>
<s> there is a bustle in court <\s>
<s> speaking to the reporters gentlemen of the press i think that the name of the female witness should not be reported <\s>
<s> the reporters bow their acquiescence <\s>
<s> to ruth who is staring in the direction in which falder has disappeared do you understand your name will not be mentioned <\s>
<s> pulling her sleeve the judge is speaking to you <\s>
<s> ruth turns stares at the judge and turns away <\s>
<s> i shall sit rather late to day <\s>
<s> call the next case <\s>
<s> to a warder put up john booley <\s>
<s> to cries of witnesses in the case of booley the curtain falls <\s>
<s> act iii scene i a prison <\s>
<s> a plainly furnished room with two large barred windows overlooking the prisoners exercise yard where men in yellow clothes marked with arrows and yellow brimless caps are seen in single file at a distance of four yards from each other walking rapidly on serpentine white lines marked on the concrete floor of the yard <\s>
<s> two warders in blue uniforms with peaked caps and swords are stationed amongst them <\s>
<s> the room has distempered walls a bookcase with numerous official looking books a cupboard between the windows a plan of the prison on the wall a writing table covered with documents <\s>
<s> it is christmas eve <\s>
<s> the governor a neat grave looking man with a trim fair moustache the eyes of a theorist and grizzled hair receding from the temples is standing close to this writing table looking at a sort of rough saw made out of a piece of metal <\s>
<s> the hand in which he holds it is gloved for two fingers are missing <\s>
<s> the chief warder wooder a tall thin military looking man of sixty with grey moustache and melancholy monkey like eyes stands very upright two paces from him <\s>
<s> with a faint abstracted smile queer looking affair mr <\s>
<s> where did you find it <\s>
<s> in his mattress sir <\s>
<s> haven't come across such a thing for two years now <\s>
<s> with curiosity had he any set plan <\s>
<s> he'd sawed his window bar about that much <\s>
<s> he holds up his thumb and finger a quarter of an inch apart the governor <\s>
<s> i'll see him this afternoon <\s>
<s> an old hand i think <\s>
<s> yes sir fourth spell of penal <\s>

<s> breaking in and breaking out that's all they think about <\s>

<s> i want to see him about his eyes <\s>
<s> curious thing sir they seem to know when there's one of these tries at escape going on <\s>

<s> i don't know of anything <\s>
<s> by the way will you dine with us on christmas day <\s>

<s> can't help liking a man who tries to escape <\s>

<s> the room has distempered walls a bookcase with numerous official looking books a cupboard between the windows a plan of the prison on the wall a writing table covered with documents <\s>
<s> it is christmas eve <\s>
<s> the governor a neat grave looking man with a trim fair moustache the eyes of a theorist and grizzled hair receding from the temples is standing close to this writing table looking at a sort of rough saw made out of a piece of metal <\s>
<s> the hand in which he holds it is gloved for two fingers are missing <\s>
<s> the chief warder wooder a tall thin military looking man of sixty with grey moustache and melancholy monkey like eyes stands very upright two paces from him <\s>
<s> with a faint abstracted smile queer looking affair mr <\s>
<s> where did you find it <\s>
<s> in his mattress sir <\s>
<s> haven't come across such a thing for two years now <\s>
<s> with curiosity had he any set plan <\s>
<s> he'd sawed his window bar about that much <\s>
<s> he holds up his thumb and finger a quarter of an inch apart the governor <\s>
<s> i'll see him this afternoon <\s>
<s> an old hand i think <\s>
<s> yes sir fourth spell of penal <\s>
<s> you'd think an old lag like him would have had more sense by now <\s>
<s> with pitying contempt occupied his mind he said <\s>
<s> breaking in and breaking out that's all they think about <\s>
<s> next him again there's that young fellow falder star class and next him old clipton <\s>
<s> i want to see him about his eyes <\s>
<s> curious thing sir they seem to know when there's one of these tries at escape going on <\s>
<s> it makes them restive there's a regular wave going through them just now <\s>
<s> meditatively odd things those waves <\s>
<s> turning to look at the prisoners exercising seem quiet enough out here <\s>
<s> that irishman o'cleary began banging on his door this morning <\s>
<s> little thing like that's quite enough to upset the whole lot <\s>
<s> they're just like dumb animals at times <\s>
<s> i've seen it with horses before thunder it'll run right through cavalry lines <\s>
<s> the prison chaplain has entered <\s>
<s> he is a dark haired ascetic man in clerical undress with a peculiarly steady tight lipped face and slow cultured speech <\s>
<s> holding up the saw seen this miller <\s>
<s> do for the museum eh <\s>
<s> he goes to the cupboard and opens it displaying to view a number of quaint ropes hooks and metal tools with labels tied on them that'll do thanks mr <\s>
<s> saluting thank you sir <\s>
<s> he goes out the governor <\s>
<s> account for the state of the men last day or two miller <\s>
<s> seems going through the whole place <\s>
<s> i don't know of anything <\s>
<s> by the way will you dine with us on christmas day <\s>
<s> worries me to feel the men discontented <\s>
<s> gazing at the saw have to punish this poor devil <\s>
<s> can't help liking a man who tries to escape <\s>
<s> he places the saw in his pocket and locks the cupboard again the chaplain <\s>
<s> extraordinary perverted will power some of them <\s>
<s> nothing to be done till it's broken <\s>
<s> and not much afterwards i'm afraid <\s>
<s> ground too hard for golf <\s>
<s> wooder comes in again <\s>
<s> visitor who's been seeing q 3007 asks to speak to you sir <\s>
<s> i told him it wasn't usual <\s>
<s> shall i put him off sir <\s>
<s> wooder motions to some one without and as the visitor comes in withdraws <\s>
<s> the visitor is cokeson who is attired in a thick overcoat to the knees woollen gloves and carries a top hat <\s>
<s> i'm sorry to trouble you <\s>
<s> i've been talking to the young man <\s>
<s> we have a good many here <\s>
<s> name of falder forgery <\s>
<s> producing a card and handing it to the governor firm of james and walter how <\s>
<s> well known in the law <\s>
<s> receiving the card with a faint smile what do you want to see me about sir <\s>
<s> suddenly seeing the prisoners at exercise why <\s>
<s> yes we have that privilege from here my office is being done up <\s>
<s> sitting down at his table now please <\s>
<s> dragging his eyes with difficulty from the window i wanted to say a word to you i shan't keep you long <\s>
<s> confidentially fact is i oughtn't to be here by rights <\s>
<s> his sister came to me he's got no father and mother and she was in some distress <\s>
<s> my husband won't let me go and see him she said says he's disgraced the family <\s>
<s> and his other sister she said is an invalid <\s>
<s> it is said however that you were carried away by your emotions <\s>
<s> the story has been told here to day of your relations with this er mrs <\s>
<s> honeywill on that story both the defence and the plea for mercy were in effect based <\s>
<s> now what is that story <\s>
<s> it is that you a young man and she a young woman unhappily married had formed an attachment which you both say with what truth i am unable to gauge had not yet resulted in immoral relations but which you both admit was about to result in such relationship <\s>
<s> your counsel has made an attempt to palliate this on the ground that the woman is in what he describes i think as a hopeless position <\s>
<s> as to that i can express no opinion <\s>
<s> she is a married woman and the fact is patent that you committed this crime with the view of furthering an immoral design <\s>
<s> now however i might wish i am not able to justify to my conscience a plea for mercy which has a basis inimical to morality <\s>
<s> it is vitiated ab initio and would if successful free you for the completion of this immoral project <\s>
<s> your counsel has made an attempt to trace your offence back to what he seems to suggest is a defect in the marriage law he has made an attempt also to show that to punish you with further imprisonment would be unjust <\s>
<s> i do not follow him in these flights <\s>
<s> the law is what it is a majestic edifice sheltering all of us each stone of which rests on another <\s>
<s> i am concerned only with its administration <\s>
<s> the crime you have committed is a very serious one <\s>
<s> i cannot feel it in accordance with my duty to society to exercise the powers i have in your favour <\s>
<s> you will go to penal servitude for three years <\s>
<s> falder who throughout the judge's speech has looked at him steadily lets his head fall forward on his breast <\s>
<s> ruth starts up from her seat as he is taken out by the warders <\s>
<s> there is a bustle in court <\s>
<s> speaking to the reporters gentlemen of the press i think that the name of the female witness should not be reported <\s>
<s> the reporters bow their acquiescence <\s>
<s> to ruth who is staring in the direction in which falder has disappeared do you understand your name will not be mentioned <\s>
<s> pulling her sleeve the judge is speaking to you <\s>
<s> ruth turns stares at the judge and turns away <\s>
<s> i shall sit rather late to day <\s>
<s> call the next case <\s>
<s> to a warder put up john booley <\s>
<s> to cries of witnesses in the case of booley the curtain falls <\s>

<s> receiving the card with a faint smile what do you want to see me about sir <\s>
<s> suddenly seeing the prisoners at exercise why <\s>
<s> yes we have that privilege from here my office is being done up <\s>
<s> sitting down at his table now please <\s>
<s> dragging his eyes with difficulty from the window i wanted to say a word to you i shan't keep you long <\s>
<s> confidentially fact is i oughtn't to be here by rights <\s>
<s> his sister came to me he's got no father and mother and she was in some distress <\s>
<s> my husband won't let me go and see him she said says he's disgraced the family <\s>
<s> and his other sister she said is an invalid <\s>
<s> it is said however that you were carried away by your emotions <\s>
<s> the story has been told here to day of your relations with this er mrs <\s>
<s> honeywill on that story both the defence and the plea for mercy were in effect based <\s>
<s> now what is that story <\s>
<s> it is that you a young man and she a young woman unhappily married had formed an attachment which you both say with what truth i am unable to gauge had not yet resulted in immoral relations but which you both admit was about to result in such relationship <\s>
<s> your counsel has made an attempt to palliate this on the ground that the woman is in what he describes i think as a hopeless position <\s>
<s> as to that i can express no opinion <\s>
<s> she is a married woman and the fact is patent that you committed this crime with the view of furthering an immoral design <\s>
<s> now however i might wish i am not able to justify to my conscience a plea for mercy which has a basis inimical to morality <\s>
<s> it is vitiated ab initio and would if successful free you for the completion of this immoral project <\s>
<s> your counsel has made an attempt to trace your offence back to what he seems to suggest is a defect in the marriage law he has made an attempt also to show that to punish you with further imprisonment would be unjust <\s>
<s> i do not follow him in these flights <\s>
<s> the law is what it is a majestic edifice sheltering all of us each stone of which rests on another <\s>
<s> i am concerned only with its administration <\s>
<s> the crime you have committed is a very serious one <\s>
<s> i cannot feel it in accordance with my duty to society to exercise the powers i have in your favour <\s>
<s> you will go to penal servitude for three years <\s>
<s> falder who throughout the judge's speech has looked at him steadily lets his head fall forward on his breast <\s>
<s> ruth starts up from her seat as he is taken out by the warders <\s>
<s> there is a bustle in court <\s>
<s> speaking to the reporters gentlemen of the press i think that the name of the female witness should not be reported <\s>
<s> the reporters bow their acquiescence <\s>
<s> to ruth who is staring in the direction in which falder has disappeared do you understand your name will not be mentioned <\s>
<s> pulling her sleeve the judge is speaking to you <\s>
<s> ruth turns stares at the judge and turns away <\s>
<s> i shall sit rather late to day <\s>
<s> call the next case <\s>
<s> to a warder put up john booley <\s>
<s> to cries of witnesses in the case of booley the curtain falls <\s>
<s> act iii scene i a prison <\s>
<s> a plainly furnished room with two large barred windows overlooking the prisoners exercise yard where men in yellow clothes marked with arrows and yellow brimless caps are seen in single file at a distance of four yards from each other walking rapidly on serpentine white lines marked on the concrete floor of the yard <\s>
<s> two warders in blue uniforms with peaked caps and swords are stationed amongst them <\s>
<s> the room has distempered walls a bookcase with numerous official looking books a cupboard between the windows a plan of the prison on the wall a writing table covered with documents <\s>
<s> it is christmas eve <\s>
<s> the governor a neat grave looking man with a trim fair moustache the eyes of a theorist and grizzled hair receding from the temples is standing close to this writing table looking at a sort of rough saw made out of a piece of metal <\s>
<s> the hand in which he holds it is gloved for two fingers are missing <\s>
<s> the chief warder wooder a tall thin military looking man of sixty with grey moustache and melancholy monkey like eyes stands very upright two paces from him <\s>
<s> with a faint abstracted smile queer looking affair mr <\s>
<s> where did you find it <\s>
<s> in his mattress sir <\s>
<s> haven't come across such a thing for two years now <\s>
<s> with curiosity had he any set plan <\s>
<s> he'd sawed his window bar about that much <\s>
<s> he holds up his thumb and finger a quarter of an inch apart the governor <\s>
<s> i'll see him this afternoon <\s>
<s> an old hand i think <\s>
<s> yes sir fourth spell of penal <\s>
<s> you'd think an old lag like him would have had more sense by now <\s>
<s> with pitying contempt occupied his mind he said <\s>
<s> breaking in and breaking out that's all they think about <\s>
<s> next him again there's that young fellow falder star class and next him old clipton <\s>
<s> i want to see him about his eyes <\s>
<s> curious thing sir they seem to know when there's one of these tries at escape going on <\s>
<s> it makes them restive there's a regular wave going through them just now <\s>
<s> meditatively odd things those waves <\s>
<s> turning to look at the prisoners exercising seem quiet enough out here <\s>
<s> that irishman o'cleary began banging on his door this morning <\s>

<s> they're just like dumb animals at times <\s>
<s> i've seen it with horses before thunder it'll run right through cavalry lines <\s>

<s> holding up the saw seen this miller <\s>
<s> do for the museum eh <\s>

<s> saluting thank you sir <\s>
<s> he goes out the governor <\s>
<s> account for the state of the men last day or two miller <\s>
<s> seems going through the whole place <\s>
<s> i don't know of anything <\s>
<s> by the way will you dine with us on christmas day <\s>
<s> worries me to feel the men discontented <\s>
<s> gazing at the saw have to punish this poor devil <\s>
<s> can't help liking a man who tries to escape <\s>
<s> he places the saw in his pocket and locks the cupboard again the chaplain <\s>
<s> extraordinary perverted will power some of them <\s>
<s> nothing to be done till it's broken <\s>
<s> and not much afterwards i'm afraid <\s>
<s> ground too hard for golf <\s>

<s> suddenly seeing the prisoners at exercise why <\s>
<s> yes we have that privilege from here my office is being done up <\s>
<s> sitting down at his table now please <\s>
<s> dragging his eyes with difficulty from the window i wanted to say a word to you i shan't keep you long <\s>
<s> confidentially fact is i oughtn't to be here by rights <\s>
<s> his sister came to me he's got no father and mother and she was in some distress <\s>
<s> my husband won't let me go and see him she said says he's disgraced the family <\s>
<s> and his other sister she said is an invalid <\s>
<s> it is said however that you were carried away by your emotions <\s>
<s> the story has been told here to day of your relations with this er mrs <\s>
<s> honeywill on that story both the defence and the plea for mercy were in effect based <\s>
<s> now what is that story <\s>
<s> it is that you a young man and she a young woman unhappily married had formed an attachment which you both say with what truth i am unable to gauge had not yet resulted in immoral relations but which you both admit was about to result in such relationship <\s>
<s> your counsel has made an attempt to palliate this on the ground that the woman is in what he describes i think as a hopeless position <\s>
<s> as to that i can express no opinion <\s>
<s> she is a married woman and the fact is patent that you committed this crime with the view of furthering an immoral design <\s>
<s> now however i might wish i am not able to justify to my conscience a plea for mercy which has a basis inimical to morality <\s>
<s> it is vitiated ab initio and would if successful free you for the completion of this immoral project <\s>
<s> your counsel has made an attempt to trace your offence back to what he seems to suggest is a defect in the marriage law he has made an attempt also to show that to punish you with further imprisonment would be unjust <\s>
<s> i do not follow him in these flights <\s>
<s> the law is what it is a majestic edifice sheltering all of us each stone of which rests on another <\s>
<s> i am concerned only with its administration <\s>
<s> the crime you have committed is a very serious one <\s>
<s> i cannot feel it in accordance with my duty to society to exercise the powers i have in your favour <\s>
<s> you will go to penal servitude for three years <\s>
<s> falder who throughout the judge's speech has looked at him steadily lets his head fall forward on his breast <\s>
<s> ruth starts up from her seat as he is taken out by the warders <\s>
<s> there is a bustle in court <\s>
<s> speaking to the reporters gentlemen of the press i think that the name of the female witness should not be reported <\s>
<s> the reporters bow their acquiescence <\s>
<s> to ruth who is staring in the direction in which falder has disappeared do you understand your name will not be mentioned <\s>
<s> pulling her sleeve the judge is speaking to you <\s>
<s> ruth turns stares at the judge and turns away <\s>
<s> i shall sit rather late to day <\s>
<s> call the next case <\s>
<s> to a warder put up john booley <\s>
<s> to cries of witnesses in the case of booley the curtain falls <\s>

<s> it is that you a young man and she a young woman unhappily married had formed an attachment which you both say with what truth i am unable to gauge had not yet resulted in immoral relations but which you both admit was about to result in such relationship <\s>
<s> your counsel has made an attempt to palliate this on the ground that the woman is in what he describes i think as a hopeless position <\s>
<s> as to that i can express no opinion <\s>
<s> she is a married woman and the fact is patent that you committed this crime with the view of furthering an immoral design <\s>
<s> now however i might wish i am not able to justify to my conscience a plea for mercy which has a basis inimical to morality <\s>
<s> it is vitiated ab initio and would if successful free you for the completion of this immoral project <\s>
<s> your counsel has made an attempt to trace your offence back to what he seems to suggest is a defect in the marriage law he has made an attempt also to show that to punish you with further imprisonment would be unjust <\s>
<s> i do not follow him in these flights <\s>
<s> the law is what it is a majestic edifice sheltering all of us each stone of which rests on another <\s>
<s> i am concerned only with its administration <\s>
<s> the crime you have committed is a very serious one <\s>
<s> i cannot feel it in accordance with my duty to society to exercise the powers i have in your favour <\s>
<s> you will go to penal servitude for three years <\s>
<s> falder who throughout the judge's speech has looked at him steadily lets his head fall forward on his breast <\s>
<s> ruth starts up from her seat as he is taken out by the warders <\s>
<s> there is a bustle in court <\s>
<s> speaking to the reporters gentlemen of the press i think that the name of the female witness should not be reported <\s>
<s> the reporters bow their acquiescence <\s>
<s> to ruth who is staring in the direction in which falder has disappeared do you understand your name will not be mentioned <\s>
<s> pulling her sleeve the judge is speaking to you <\s>
<s> ruth turns stares at the judge and turns away <\s>
<s> i shall sit rather late to day <\s>
<s> call the next case <\s>
<s> to a warder put up john booley <\s>
<s> to cries of witnesses in the case of booley the curtain falls <\s>
<s> act iii scene i a prison <\s>
<s> a plainly furnished room with two large barred windows overlooking the prisoners exercise yard where men in yellow clothes marked with arrows and yellow brimless caps are seen in single file at a distance of four yards from each other walking rapidly on serpentine white lines marked on the concrete floor of the yard <\s>
<s> two warders in blue uniforms with peaked caps and swords are stationed amongst them <\s>
<s> the room has distempered walls a bookcase with numerous official looking books a cupboard between the windows a plan of the prison on the wall a writing table covered with documents <\s>
<s> it is christmas eve <\s>
<s> the governor a neat grave looking man with a trim fair moustache the eyes of a theorist and grizzled hair receding from the temples is standing close to this writing table looking at a sort of rough saw made out of a piece of metal <\s>
<s> the hand in which he holds it is gloved for two fingers are missing <\s>
<s> the chief warder wooder a tall thin military looking man of sixty with grey moustache and melancholy monkey like eyes stands very upright two paces from him <\s>
<s> with a faint abstracted smile queer looking affair mr <\s>
<s> where did you find it <\s>
<s> in his mattress sir <\s>
<s> haven't come across such a thing for two years now <\s>
<s> with curiosity had he any set plan <\s>
<s> he'd sawed his window bar about that much <\s>
<s> he holds up his thumb and finger a quarter of an inch apart the governor <\s>
<s> i'll see him this afternoon <\s>
<s> an old hand i think <\s>
<s> yes sir fourth spell of penal <\s>
<s> you'd think an old lag like him would have had more sense by now <\s>
<s> with pitying contempt occupied his mind he said <\s>
<s> breaking in and breaking out that's all they think about <\s>
<s> next him again there's that young fellow falder star class and next him old clipton <\s>
<s> i want to see him about his eyes <\s>
<s> curious thing sir they seem to know when there's one of these tries at escape going on <\s>
<s> it makes them restive there's a regular wave going through them just now <\s>
<s> meditatively odd things those waves <\s>
<s> turning to look at the prisoners exercising seem quiet enough out here <\s>
<s> that irishman o'cleary began banging on his door this morning <\s>
<s> little thing like that's quite enough to upset the whole lot <\s>
<s> they're just like dumb animals at times <\s>
<s> i've seen it with horses before thunder it'll run right through cavalry lines <\s>
<s> the prison chaplain has entered <\s>
<s> he is a dark haired ascetic man in clerical undress with a peculiarly steady tight lipped face and slow cultured speech <\s>
<s> holding up the saw seen this miller <\s>
<s> do for the museum eh <\s>
<s> he goes to the cupboard and opens it displaying to view a number of quaint ropes hooks and metal tools with labels tied on them that'll do thanks mr <\s>
<s> saluting thank you sir <\s>
<s> he goes out the governor <\s>
<s> account for the state of the men last day or two miller <\s>
<s> seems going through the whole place <\s>
<s> i don't know of anything <\s>
<s> by the way will you dine with us on christmas day <\s>
<s> worries me to feel the men discontented <\s>
<s> gazing at the saw have to punish this poor devil <\s>
<s> can't help liking a man who tries to escape <\s>
<s> he places the saw in his pocket and locks the cupboard again the chaplain <\s>
<s> extraordinary perverted will power some of them <\s>
<s> nothing to be done till it's broken <\s>
<s> and not much afterwards i'm afraid <\s>
<s> ground too hard for golf <\s>
<s> wooder comes in again <\s>
<s> visitor who's been seeing q 3007 asks to speak to you sir <\s>
<s> i told him it wasn't usual <\s>
<s> shall i put him off sir <\s>

<s> dragging his eyes with difficulty from the window i wanted to say a word to you i shan't keep you long <\s>
<s> confidentially fact is i oughtn't to be here by rights <\s>
<s> his sister came to me he's got no father and mother and she was in some distress <\s>
<s> my husband won't let me go and see him she said says he's disgraced the family <\s>
<s> and his other sister she said is an invalid <\s>
<s> it is said however that you were carried away by your emotions <\s>
<s> the story has been told here to day of your relations with this er mrs <\s>
<s> honeywill on that story both the defence and the plea for mercy were in effect based <\s>
<s> now what is that story <\s>
<s> it is that you a young man and she a young woman unhappily married had formed an attachment which you both say with what truth i am unable to gauge had not yet resulted in immoral relations but which you both admit was about to result in such relationship <\s>
<s> your counsel has made an attempt to palliate this on the ground that the woman is in what he describes i think as a hopeless position <\s>
<s> as to that i can express no opinion <\s>
<s> she is a married woman and the fact is patent that you committed this crime with the view of furthering an immoral design <\s>
<s> now however i might wish i am not able to justify to my conscience a plea for mercy which has a basis inimical to morality <\s>
<s> it is vitiated ab initio and would if successful free you for the completion of this immoral project <\s>
<s> your counsel has made an attempt to trace your offence back to what he seems to suggest is a defect in the marriage law he has made an attempt also to show that to punish you with further imprisonment would be unjust <\s>
<s> i do not follow him in these flights <\s>
<s> the law is what it is a majestic edifice sheltering all of us each stone of which rests on another <\s>
<s> i am concerned only with its administration <\s>
<s> the crime you have committed is a very serious one <\s>
<s> i cannot feel it in accordance with my duty to society to exercise the powers i have in your favour <\s>
<s> you will go to penal servitude for three years <\s>
<s> falder who throughout the judge's speech has looked at him steadily lets his head fall forward on his breast <\s>
<s> ruth starts up from her seat as he is taken out by the warders <\s>
<s> there is a bustle in court <\s>
<s> speaking to the reporters gentlemen of the press i think that the name of the female witness should not be reported <\s>
<s> the reporters bow their acquiescence <\s>

<s> act iii scene i a prison <\s>
<s> a plainly furnished room with two large barred windows overlooking the prisoners exercise yard where men in yellow clothes marked with arrows and yellow brimless caps are seen in single file at a distance of four yards from each other walking rapidly on serpentine white lines marked on the concrete floor of the yard <\s>

<s> the law is what it is a majestic edifice sheltering all of us each stone of which rests on another <\s>
<s> i am concerned only with its administration <\s>
<s> the crime you have committed is a very serious one <\s>
<s> i cannot feel it in accordance with my duty to society to exercise the powers i have in your favour <\s>
<s> you will go to penal servitude for three years <\s>
<s> falder who throughout the judge's speech has looked at him steadily lets his head fall forward on his breast <\s>
<s> ruth starts up from her seat as he is taken out by the warders <\s>
<s> there is a bustle in court <\s>
<s> speaking to the reporters gentlemen of the press i think that the name of the female witness should not be reported <\s>
<s> the reporters bow their acquiescence <\s>
<s> to ruth who is staring in the direction in which falder has disappeared do you understand your name will not be mentioned <\s>
<s> pulling her sleeve the judge is speaking to you <\s>
<s> ruth turns stares at the judge and turns away <\s>
<s> i shall sit rather late to day <\s>
<s> call the next case <\s>
<s> to a warder put up john booley <\s>
<s> to cries of witnesses in the case of booley the curtain falls <\s>
<s> act iii scene i a prison <\s>
<s> a plainly furnished room with two large barred windows overlooking the prisoners exercise yard where men in yellow clothes marked with arrows and yellow brimless caps are seen in single file at a distance of four yards from each other walking rapidly on serpentine white lines marked on the concrete floor of the yard <\s>
<s> two warders in blue uniforms with peaked caps and swords are stationed amongst them <\s>
<s> the room has distempered walls a bookcase with numerous official looking books a cupboard between the windows a plan of the prison on the wall a writing table covered with documents <\s>
<s> it is christmas eve <\s>
<s> the governor a neat grave looking man with a trim fair moustache the eyes of a theorist and grizzled hair receding from the temples is standing close to this writing table looking at a sort of rough saw made out of a piece of metal <\s>
<s> the hand in which he holds it is gloved for two fingers are missing <\s>
<s> the chief warder wooder a tall thin military looking man of sixty with grey moustache and melancholy monkey like eyes stands very upright two paces from him <\s>
<s> with a faint abstracted smile queer looking affair mr <\s>
<s> where did you find it <\s>
<s> in his mattress sir <\s>
<s> haven't come across such a thing for two years now <\s>
<s> with curiosity had he any set plan <\s>
<s> he'd sawed his window bar about that much <\s>
<s> he holds up his thumb and finger a quarter of an inch apart the governor <\s>
<s> i'll see him this afternoon <\s>
<s> an old hand i think <\s>
<s> yes sir fourth spell of penal <\s>
<s> you'd think an old lag like him would have had more sense by now <\s>
<s> with pitying contempt occupied his mind he said <\s>
<s> breaking in and breaking out that's all they think about <\s>
<s> next him again there's that young fellow falder star class and next him old clipton <\s>
<s> i want to see him about his eyes <\s>
<s> curious thing sir they seem to know when there's one of these tries at escape going on <\s>
<s> it makes them restive there's a regular wave going through them just now <\s>
<s> meditatively odd things those waves <\s>
<s> turning to look at the prisoners exercising seem quiet enough out here <\s>
<s> that irishman o'cleary began banging on his door this morning <\s>
<s> little thing like that's quite enough to upset the whole lot <\s>
<s> they're just like dumb animals at times <\s>
<s> i've seen it with horses before thunder it'll run right through cavalry lines <\s>
<s> the prison chaplain has entered <\s>
<s> he is a dark haired ascetic man in clerical undress with a peculiarly steady tight lipped face and slow cultured speech <\s>
<s> holding up the saw seen this miller <\s>
<s> do for the museum eh <\s>
<s> he goes to the cupboard and opens it displaying to view a number of quaint ropes hooks and metal tools with labels tied on them that'll do thanks mr <\s>
<s> saluting thank you sir <\s>
<s> he goes out the governor <\s>
<s> account for the state of the men last day or two miller <\s>
<s> seems going through the whole place <\s>
<s> i don't know of anything <\s>
<s> by the way will you dine with us on christmas day <\s>
<s> worries me to feel the men discontented <\s>
<s> gazing at the saw have to punish this poor devil <\s>
<s> can't help liking a man who tries to escape <\s>
<s> he places the saw in his pocket and locks the cupboard again the chaplain <\s>
<s> extraordinary perverted will power some of them <\s>
<s> nothing to be done till it's broken <\s>
<s> and not much afterwards i'm afraid <\s>
<s> ground too hard for golf <\s>
<s> wooder comes in again <\s>
<s> visitor who's been seeing q 3007 asks to speak to you sir <\s>
<s> i told him it wasn't usual <\s>
<s> shall i put him off sir <\s>
<s> wooder motions to some one without and as the visitor comes in withdraws <\s>
<s> the visitor is cokeson who is attired in a thick overcoat to the knees woollen gloves and carries a top hat <\s>
<s> i'm sorry to trouble you <\s>

<s> name of falder forgery <\s>

<s> well known in the law <\s>

<s> suddenly seeing the prisoners at exercise why <\s>

<s> sitting down at his table now please <\s>
<s> dragging his eyes with difficulty from the window i wanted to say a word to you i shan't keep you long <\s>
<s> confidentially fact is i oughtn't to be here by rights <\s>
<s> his sister came to me he's got no father and mother and she was in some distress <\s>
<s> my husband won't let me go and see him she said says he's disgraced the family <\s>
<s> and his other sister she said is an invalid <\s>
<s> it is said however that you were carried away by your emotions <\s>
<s> the story has been told here to day of your relations with this er mrs <\s>
<s> honeywill on that story both the defence and the plea for mercy were in effect based <\s>
<s> now what is that story <\s>
<s> it is that you a young man and she a young woman unhappily married had formed an attachment which you both say with what truth i am unable to gauge had not yet resulted in immoral relations but which you both admit was about to result in such relationship <\s>
<s> your counsel has made an attempt to palliate this on the ground that the woman is in what he describes i think as a hopeless position <\s>
<s> as to that i can express no opinion <\s>

<s> his sister came to me he's got no father and mother and she was in some distress <\s>
<s> my husband won't let me go and see him she said says he's disgraced the family <\s>
<s> and his other sister she said is an invalid <\s>
<s> it is said however that you were carried away by your emotions <\s>
<s> the story has been told here to day of your relations with this er mrs <\s>
<s> honeywill on that story both the defence and the plea for mercy were in effect based <\s>
<s> now what is that story <\s>
<s> it is that you a young man and she a young woman unhappily married had formed an attachment which you both say with what truth i am unable to gauge had not yet resulted in immoral relations but which you both admit was about to result in such relationship <\s>
<s> your counsel has made an attempt to palliate this on the ground that the woman is in what he describes i think as a hopeless position <\s>
<s> as to that i can express no opinion <\s>
<s> she is a married woman and the fact is patent that you committed this crime with the view of furthering an immoral design <\s>
<s> now however i might wish i am not able to justify to my conscience a plea for mercy which has a basis inimical to morality <\s>
<s> it is vitiated ab initio and would if successful free you for the completion of this immoral project <\s>
<s> your counsel has made an attempt to trace your offence back to what he seems to suggest is a defect in the marriage law he has made an attempt also to show that to punish you with further imprisonment would be unjust <\s>
<s> i do not follow him in these flights <\s>
<s> the law is what it is a majestic edifice sheltering all of us each stone of which rests on another <\s>
<s> i am concerned only with its administration <\s>
<s> the crime you have committed is a very serious one <\s>
<s> i cannot feel it in accordance with my duty to society to exercise the powers i have in your favour <\s>
<s> you will go to penal servitude for three years <\s>
<s> falder who throughout the judge's speech has looked at him steadily lets his head fall forward on his breast <\s>
<s> ruth starts up from her seat as he is taken out by the warders <\s>
<s> there is a bustle in court <\s>
<s> speaking to the reporters gentlemen of the press i think that the name of the female witness should not be reported <\s>
<s> the reporters bow their acquiescence <\s>
<s> to ruth who is staring in the direction in which falder has disappeared do you understand your name will not be mentioned <\s>

<s> act iii scene i a prison <\s>
<s> a plainly furnished room with two large barred windows overlooking the prisoners exercise yard where men in yellow clothes marked with arrows and yellow brimless caps are seen in single file at a distance of four yards from each other walking rapidly on serpentine white lines marked on the concrete floor of the yard <\s>
<s> two warders in blue uniforms with peaked caps and swords are stationed amongst them <\s>
<s> the room has distempered walls a bookcase with numerous official looking books a cupboard between the windows a plan of the prison on the wall a writing table covered with documents <\s>
<s> it is christmas eve <\s>
<s> the governor a neat grave looking man with a trim fair moustache the eyes of a theorist and grizzled hair receding from the temples is standing close to this writing table looking at a sort of rough saw made out of a piece of metal <\s>
<s> the hand in which he holds it is gloved for two fingers are missing <\s>

<s> act iii scene i a prison <\s>
<s> a plainly furnished room with two large barred windows overlooking the prisoners exercise yard where men in yellow clothes marked with arrows and yellow brimless caps are seen in single file at a distance of four yards from each other walking rapidly on serpentine white lines marked on the concrete floor of the yard <\s>
<s> two warders in blue uniforms with peaked caps and swords are stationed amongst them <\s>
<s> the room has distempered walls a bookcase with numerous official looking books a cupboard between the windows a plan of the prison on the wall a writing table covered with documents <\s>
<s> it is christmas eve <\s>
<s> the governor a neat grave looking man with a trim fair moustache the eyes of a theorist and grizzled hair receding from the temples is standing close to this writing table looking at a sort of rough saw made out of a piece of metal <\s>
<s> the hand in which he holds it is gloved for two fingers are missing <\s>
<s> the chief warder wooder a tall thin military looking man of sixty with grey moustache and melancholy monkey like eyes stands very upright two paces from him <\s>
<s> with a faint abstracted smile queer looking affair mr <\s>
<s> where did you find it <\s>
<s> in his mattress sir <\s>
<s> haven't come across such a thing for two years now <\s>
<s> with curiosity had he any set plan <\s>
<s> he'd sawed his window bar about that much <\s>
<s> he holds up his thumb and finger a quarter of an inch apart the governor <\s>
<s> i'll see him this afternoon <\s>
<s> an old hand i think <\s>
<s> yes sir fourth spell of penal <\s>
<s> you'd think an old lag like him would have had more sense by now <\s>
<s> with pitying contempt occupied his mind he said <\s>
<s> breaking in and breaking out that's all they think about <\s>
<s> next him again there's that young fellow falder star class and next him old clipton <\s>
<s> i want to see him about his eyes <\s>
<s> curious thing sir they seem to know when there's one of these tries at escape going on <\s>
<s> it makes them restive there's a regular wave going through them just now <\s>
<s> meditatively odd things those waves <\s>
<s> turning to look at the prisoners exercising seem quiet enough out here <\s>
<s> that irishman o'cleary began banging on his door this morning <\s>
<s> little thing like that's quite enough to upset the whole lot <\s>
<s> they're just like dumb animals at times <\s>
<s> i've seen it with horses before thunder it'll run right through cavalry lines <\s>
<s> the prison chaplain has entered <\s>
<s> he is a dark haired ascetic man in clerical undress with a peculiarly steady tight lipped face and slow cultured speech <\s>
<s> holding up the saw seen this miller <\s>
<s> do for the museum eh <\s>
<s> he goes to the cupboard and opens it displaying to view a number of quaint ropes hooks and metal tools with labels tied on them that'll do thanks mr <\s>
<s> saluting thank you sir <\s>
<s> he goes out the governor <\s>
<s> account for the state of the men last day or two miller <\s>
<s> seems going through the whole place <\s>
<s> i don't know of anything <\s>
<s> by the way will you dine with us on christmas day <\s>
<s> worries me to feel the men discontented <\s>
<s> gazing at the saw have to punish this poor devil <\s>
<s> can't help liking a man who tries to escape <\s>
<s> he places the saw in his pocket and locks the cupboard again the chaplain <\s>
<s> extraordinary perverted will power some of them <\s>
<s> nothing to be done till it's broken <\s>
<s> and not much afterwards i'm afraid <\s>
<s> ground too hard for golf <\s>
<s> wooder comes in again <\s>
<s> visitor who's been seeing q 3007 asks to speak to you sir <\s>
<s> i told him it wasn't usual <\s>
<s> shall i put him off sir <\s>
<s> wooder motions to some one without and as the visitor comes in withdraws <\s>
<s> the visitor is cokeson who is attired in a thick overcoat to the knees woollen gloves and carries a top hat <\s>
<s> i'm sorry to trouble you <\s>
<s> i've been talking to the young man <\s>
<s> we have a good many here <\s>
<s> name of falder forgery <\s>
<s> producing a card and handing it to the governor firm of james and walter how <\s>
<s> well known in the law <\s>
<s> receiving the card with a faint smile what do you want to see me about sir <\s>
<s> suddenly seeing the prisoners at exercise why <\s>
<s> yes we have that privilege from here my office is being done up <\s>
<s> sitting down at his table now please <\s>
<s> dragging his eyes with difficulty from the window i wanted to say a word to you i shan't keep you long <\s>
<s> confidentially fact is i oughtn't to be here by rights <\s>
<s> his sister came to me he's got no father and mother and she was in some distress <\s>
<s> my husband won't let me go and see him she said says he's disgraced the family <\s>
<s> and his other sister she said is an invalid <\s>
<s> it is said however that you were carried away by your emotions <\s>
<s> the story has been told here to day of your relations with this er mrs <\s>
<s> honeywill on that story both the defence and the plea for mercy were in effect based <\s>
<s> now what is that story <\s>
<s> it is that you a young man and she a young woman unhappily married had formed an attachment which you both say with what truth i am unable to gauge had not yet resulted in immoral relations but which you both admit was about to result in such relationship <\s>
<s> your counsel has made an attempt to palliate this on the ground that the woman is in what he describes i think as a hopeless position <\s>
<s> as to that i can express no opinion <\s>
<s> she is a married woman and the fact is patent that you committed this crime with the view of furthering an immoral design <\s>
<s> now however i might wish i am not able to justify to my conscience a plea for mercy which has a basis inimical to morality <\s>
<s> it is vitiated ab initio and would if successful free you for the completion of this immoral project <\s>
<s> your counsel has made an attempt to trace your offence back to what he seems to suggest is a defect in the marriage law he has made an attempt also to show that to punish you with further imprisonment would be unjust <\s>
<s> i do not follow him in these flights <\s>
<s> the law is what it is a majestic edifice sheltering all of us each stone of which rests on another <\s>
<s> i am concerned only with its administration <\s>
<s> the crime you have committed is a very serious one <\s>
<s> i cannot feel it in accordance with my duty to society to exercise the powers i have in your favour <\s>
<s> you will go to penal servitude for three years <\s>
<s> falder who throughout the judge's speech has looked at him steadily lets his head fall forward on his breast <\s>
<s> ruth starts up from her seat as he is taken out by the warders <\s>
<s> there is a bustle in court <\s>
<s> speaking to the reporters gentlemen of the press i think that the name of the female witness should not be reported <\s>
<s> the reporters bow their acquiescence <\s>
<s> to ruth who is staring in the direction in which falder has disappeared do you understand your name will not be mentioned <\s>
<s> pulling her sleeve the judge is speaking to you <\s>
<s> ruth turns stares at the judge and turns away <\s>
<s> i shall sit rather late to day <\s>
<s> call the next case <\s>
<s> to a warder put up john booley <\s>
